Suddenly, Zhang Shanfeng said, “Chen Ping'an, some things, friends can’t help with; you can only figure them out on your own, bit by bit.” 

The first time he descended the mountain and ventured out, as an outsider disciple of Longhu Mountain, he had a tough time almost not making it through. Eventually, he steeled himself and went straight to Baoping Continent, where he met Chen Ping'an and Xu Yuanxia, slowly opening up his heart and even realizing a clumsy set of martial arts that was not meant for the stage.

Chen Ping'an lightly hummed in agreement.

The deepest inquiries of the heart were the sharpest.

At this moment, Chen Ping'an’s state of mind was, of course, far from as relaxed as his words and expression suggested.

Zhang Shanfeng pulled out a porcelain bottle from his bag. “This bottle of water elixir was given to me by a friend of my master from the Middle Earth Shenzhao. He said since you gifted me the Tianshi Seal and the Zhenwu Sword, I should return the favor.”

Chen Ping'an was taken aback. He didn’t hesitate to accept the porcelain bottle, and feeling the coolness in his palm, he couldn’t help but ask curiously, “The Water God from Shenzhao gifted this?”

The Lord of Cangyun Lake had also sent him water elixirs before. He had once seen the water elixirs from Liu Chongrun's secret collection, but compared to the bottle of Shenzhao Water Elixir in his hand, it was like comparing clouds to mud.

The book on the upside-down mountain mentioned Shenzhao as a large swamp in Middle Earth, could it be the water elixir refined from the life water of the Lord of Shenzhao?

Zhang Shanfeng nodded. “It’s indeed the Shenzhao Water Elixir, but my master said its quality isn’t too high. He mentioned that his relationship with the various Water Gods around the world is average, so he couldn't get the best elixirs.”

Chen Ping'an found this a bit amusing. What the Fire Dragon Real Man considered “the best” would indeed be the best in all of Haoran World. What he referred to as “not too high” must still be quite impressive.

Shenzhao was extremely famous in Middle Earth. Its vast waters were guarded by a deity of the upper fifth realm, and the water palace was the renowned Chenchi Palace, reputed to be the largest dragon king's lair in the world. The legends surrounding the ruins of Shenzhao were numerous; it was said that an unknown Daoist once rowed a boat on a bright moonlit night, where a flood dragon fleeing from heavenly calamity entered Shenzhao, and the chains of thunder and lightning obscured the sky. That flood dragon escaped into the Daoist's sleeve, with the Daoist casually repelling the heavenly calamity, allowing the flood dragon to avoid disaster, leading to later poetry that described, “Under the thunder, there’s nowhere to hide, it flew into the scholar’s robes.”

Chen Ping'an held the heavy bottle of water elixir and turned to Zhang Shanfeng, softly saying, “You have a good master, Zhang Shanfeng.”

Zhang Shanfeng smiled, “I’ve known that for a long time.”

Chen Ping'an chuckled, “And the old real man has a good disciple.”

Zhang Shanfeng shook his head, “Disciples like me are plentiful on the Padi Peak.”

Chen Ping'an replied, “I don’t see many.”

Zhang Shanfeng’s face lit up with a smile, “Just saying some big truths.”

Chen Ping'an pulled the young Daoist into an embrace, and Zhang Shanfeng bent down, ready to return the gesture.

They joked and laughed.

Chen Ping'an led Zhang Shanfeng into the courtyard, into the house.

Zhang Shanfeng caught sight of the green bamboo walking stick and the sword immortal on the wall, laughing, “Same old, same old.”

Chen Ping'an fetched a chair for him, and they sat facing each other.

Zhang Shanfeng began sharing stories of his travels with his master through Middle Earth and Nanpusa Continent, eventually talking about Liu Xianyang, who studied under the esteemed Chen family.

Chen Ping'an quietly listened to Zhang Shanfeng’s account, his mind at peace, the ripples settling.

Zhang Shanfeng then began to recount his journey back home but suddenly noticed that the guy across from him had listened so intently that he had fallen asleep.

Zhang Shanfeng felt a bit helpless, quietly stood up, and softly left the room. After gently closing the door, he squatted under the eaves, lost in thought.

The world was strange; some people focused solely on what others had without considering why. His master said this was called a “leaf obstructing the eye” and that the stranger part of the world was that such thinking wasn’t necessarily a bad thing.

Zhang Shanfeng always felt out of place in this world, and it had little to do with levels of achievement.

He could only slowly cultivate on Padi Peak, or travel the rivers and lakes with Chen Ping'an and Xu Yuanxia, or simply be alone, facing the silent and serene mountains and waters, keeping his distance from the hustle and bustle. He wouldn’t make mistakes that harmed others, and the world wouldn’t harm him. Only then would he feel a bit better.

Zhang Shanfeng asked his master if there was a significant problem with his questioning heart.

His master said there was no issue, explaining that Confucianism was about addition—cultivating oneself, governing the family, ruling the state, bringing peace to the world—all responsibilities taken upon oneself, leading to the Middle Earth Confucian Temple. Daoism was about subtraction, where one could clearly draw lines, sever connections, and forget the self and object without worry, leading ultimately to tranquility. Buddhism transitioned from self-liberation to liberating others, gradually realizing enlightenment, with the precepts, concentration, and wisdom being stages of increase and decrease. While the three teachings seemed to differ greatly, their paths and directions were fundamentally the same, as cultivation was ultimately about the person on the road.

Zhang Shanfeng squatted on the steps, turning to glance at the closed door.

His master was right; everyone is a small universe. Once the door is closed, outsiders cannot see the true scene inside.

At that moment, inside the house, Chen Ping'an gently called out, “Zhang Shanfeng.”

Zhang Shanfeng quickly replied, “Here, just outside.”

Chen Ping'an then said, his tone slightly weary, “Then I’ll sleep a bit more. I never felt it before, but I’m a bit tired.”

Zhang Shanfeng said, “Rest well.”

Zhang Shanfeng, with his hands tucked into his sleeves, squatted in place, gently swaying back and forth, a smile on his face.

There were some children down the hill, extremely precocious. Whether they would ultimately become cultivators on the mountain wasn’t surprising.

What was truly strange was the coexistence of two extreme philosophies and characters constantly clashing without harming anyone. From Fire Dragon Real Man’s perspective, that was true cultivation and refinement.

The innate pure mindset was hard to maintain without losing it, while the acquired sincerity was challenging to find. The true essence of sincerity, when achieved, shone like the sun and glimmered like the moon.

His disciple Zhang Shanfeng and his friend Chen Ping'an had two different mindsets, requiring two different teachings.

Fire Dragon Real Man felt a bit frustrated with the Confucian sage and Qi Jingchun. Why, having recognized disciples and junior disciples separately, didn’t they pay more attention? Why let Chen Ping'an wander so far alone? Didn’t they fear he might meet misfortune or abandon his path to become a monk, or perhaps truly understand and turn to Daoism? This was something Fire Dragon Real Man couldn’t comprehend—why the Confucian sage didn’t choose to keep Chen Ping'an close, teaching him by example. It was also odd that Qi Jingchun, even if he had to die, could have done so much more with his knowledge and abilities, yet he didn’t.

Truly, each was bigger-hearted than the last.

Fire Dragon Real Man considered himself quite broad-minded, yet compared to these two scholars, he felt he still fell short.

Suddenly, Fire Dragon Real Man uttered a soft “eh,” looking around as if he encountered something perplexing, but after a moment’s thought, he lazily dismissed it.

**Between the Islands of Baijia and Cangyan.**

A carriage suspended in the water, with Li Yuan and the goddess Shen Lin standing side by side.

Shen Lin was surprised, “This person actually knows Fire Dragon Real Man?”

Li Yuan sneered, “I know that old man too.”

Shen Lin smiled, of course she recognized him, having been suppressed by Fire Dragon Real Man with water techniques for over a month at the bottom of the lake.

Though the North Julu Continent firmly believed that this old real man from Padi Peak was the world’s most skilled practitioner of fire techniques, few knew that Fire Dragon Real Man was also quite proficient with water techniques.

Shen Lin had many thoughts.

Just then, Li Yuan felt a chill on his scalp.

It turned out the old real man on the shore waved cheerfully at the carriage.

Li Yuan was about to scatter into golden light and escape but hesitated, for Fire Dragon Real Man had already appeared next to the carriage, standing on the back of a pure white steed.

Shen Lin immediately bowed respectfully, saying, “This is Shen Lin from South Xun Water Palace, I pay my respects to Fire Dragon Real Man!”

Fire Dragon Real Man was relatively polite towards this water goddess, smiling, “All things follow nature, and walk with fate; when the water flows, it naturally gathers.”

A face as delicate as shattered green glaze trembled slightly, and Shen Lin replied in a trembling voice, “Thank you for your teachings, Real Man.”

Fire Dragon Real Man smiled and remained silent, glancing at Li Yuan, “Oh, isn’t this our Li Yuan from the Jidu Temple? Wherever I go, I can always see you, Li Yuan. What a fated encounter, truly unstoppable.”

Li Yuan kept a straight face, pretending to be deaf and mute.

What’s the deal? Just because your Dao techniques are high doesn’t mean you can bully me, right?

Fire Dragon Real Man chuckled, “Li Yuan, since you’re free, why not have a chat with me?”

Li Yuan looked confused, “I’m busy, very busy.”

Fire Dragon Real Man shook his sleeve, “Oh?”

Li Yuan immediately said, “I can not be busy for now.”

An old Taoist and a young man left the carriage and walked on water.

Shen Lin used her divine powers to steer the carriage back to the summer palace.

Once Shen Lin left, Li Yuan immediately began to flatter, “Old Brother Fire Dragon, why did you come to the Water Dragon Cave Heaven as a guest without a word? Isn’t that a bit cold? Do you look down on your little brother who’s struggling?”

Fire Dragon Real Man hummed in acknowledgment.

Yes, indeed, I look down on you, Li Yuan.

Li Yuan felt it was pointless to continue the conversation.

As the esteemed Water Justice who was currently in the water, he felt as if he was in a cage, completely out of sorts.

After a long silence, they swiftly traveled through the water, their forms light and ethereal like smoke.

Fire Dragon Real Man finally spoke, “Since the establishment of the Water Dragon Sect, they haven’t treated you poorly, so why do you still act so high and mighty? Do you need to place the ancestral hall’s seats at the forefront? Always reminding the Water Dragon Sect’s past leaders that the ancestral hall is your territory? Are they just tenants? Have you lost your mind, Water Justice? Do you really think of yourself as the lord of the rivers and lakes, acting so arrogant and domineering?”

Li Yuan looked weak, “To add a crime, there are no words to argue against it. Just say whatever you want, I’ll accept it.”

Fire Dragon Real Man sneered, “Even the greatest incense offerings can’t withstand your spendthrift ways. The harmonious weather of the Water Dragon Cave Heaven is generally fine, what does it have to do with you? Isn’t Shen Lin the one working hard? Back then, when that sword immortal stole the treasures of the cave heaven’s water, why did you sit by and do nothing? Could he deceive the busy Shen Lin and the South Xun Water Palace, but not you, who’s always loitering around?”

Li Yuan pouted, “But the Water Dragon Sect hasn’t said anything.”

Fire Dragon Real Man knew there were many more complexities involved, it was not merely a matter of right or wrong. Yet in all matters of the world, one could still see the general outcome. And outcomes often served as the cause for the next cycle of karma. Just like those ripples on the lake; it’s not easy to see the vast waters, but each ripple’s rise and fall, as a cultivator, one should be able to perceive clearly, otherwise, what’s the point of cultivating?

The old real man said solemnly, “If it weren’t for my old ties with that person, do you think I would be willing to waste a word with you?”

Li Yuan sighed, no longer pretending to be foolish, his expression bleak, “I’ve watched the rise and fall of the Water Dragon Sect and the fluctuations of its incense offerings for many years, and I’ve seen too many hopes die. Now I feel it’s pointless. This generation’s sect master, Sun Jie, is decent, but what can be done? I’ve thought about refining the Jidu Temple within the Water Dragon Sect, but both of the two people I once valued couldn’t become the sect master. One was partly harmed by me and the Water Dragon Sect in partnership. The Water Dragon Sect has become my burden year after year; they brought this upon themselves.”

Fire Dragon Real Man seemed to be lamenting his misfortune and was angry at his lack of progress, “Stubborn and unyielding!”

On the mountain, painting the dragon’s eyes, nodding at the stubborn stone, playing music for a cow, communicating with a chicken, wasn’t that all knowledge?

The only difference was the immortals; they couldn’t engage in conversation at all.

Fire Dragon Real Man said, “Why not try being a decent human?”

Li Yuan, feeling humiliated and angry, retorted, “Fire Dragon Real Man, don’t bully me just because your Dao techniques are high!”

Fire Dragon Real Man pressed his palm on this young Water Justice’s head, cheerfully asking, “What’s wrong with bullying you?”

Li Yuan wanted to cry but had no tears, frowning, “Then I’ll heed your advice and behave like a good person.”

Fire Dragon Real Man lightly slapped him, sending Li Yuan tumbling into a deep pit at the bottom of the lake, laughing, “You remember the beatings but forget the lessons.”

Li Yuan lay at the bottom of the pit, playing dead.

Fire Dragon Real Man floated down into the pit, speaking solemnly, “Don’t really think of yourself as a high and mighty deity.”

Li Yuan opened his eyes, “If I’m caught between two extremes, wouldn’t that be even more distressing?”

Fire Dragon Real Man shook his head, “Self-righteousness is indeed hard to teach.”

Li Yuan rested his hands behind his head, looking woodenly, “I’m just a frog at the bottom of a well, unable to see the sky.”

Fire Dragon Real Man had quietly left without him noticing.

Li Yuan sighed, feeling he had taken a slap for nothing.

Fire Dragon Real Man slowly walked into the Fushui Island residence.

Chen Ping'an had already woken up, watching Zhang Shanfeng practice martial arts in the courtyard.

Upon seeing the old real man, Chen Ping'an was about to pay his respects, but Fire Dragon Real Man waved his hand, “Tired or not, as long as your heart is in it, I have some insight. Go inside and take a look at your third innate item. If there are no flaws, you should refine it soon. You can ponder as much as you like while climbing the mountain; that’s fine, but it doesn’t mean you should take your time. Also, moving slowly doesn’t mean you can actually dawdle. Chen Ping'an, you need to clearly differentiate between the two.”

Chen Ping'an silently noted this in his heart.

Zhang Shanfeng stopped his martial arts, and the three of them entered the house together.

Chen Ping'an carefully took out the fragments of wooden statues dedicated to the mountain top Daoist temple.

Fire Dragon Real Man waved his sleeve, and a layer of greenish gas rippled into a surface that looked like jade, smooth and bright as a mirror.

Chen Ping'an also took out the thirty-six blue bricks that paved the ground of the Daoist temple.

One hundred and twenty-two pieces of emerald green glazed tiles.

And a large bunch of bamboo branches and leaves he had gathered from that green bamboo.

Fire Dragon Real Man asked, “Have you accumulated these possessions after visiting many cave heavens and blessed lands?”

Chen Ping'an shook his head, “They were all found in one place.”

He felt embarrassed to say he had “picked them up.”

Fire Dragon Real Man looked at him oddly, “Are you a bandit?”

Chen Ping'an was about to pull out several other treasures from the mountain but had to withdraw his hand.

The lady’s round fan bought from “Daoist Sun,” and a pair of Dragon King baskets. There was also an ancient mirror gifted by Huang Shi, as well as the heart-shaped token of the Daoist gate, the jade bracelet with a reversed poem, and a tree gnarled pot.

He originally intended for the old real man to take a look and give an estimate.

Fire Dragon Real Man glanced at the pile of fragments without hastily revealing secrets, only pointing to those blue bricks, “The toughness of these bricks is comparable to the Dragon Slaying Platform that sword cultivators dream of. Because they have absorbed Daoist truths over many years, the essence of water contained within is merely superficial. If you choose to discard the blue bricks for the sake of the water essence, that would be a truly extravagant waste.”

Chen Ping'an looked at Zhang Shanfeng beside him.

Fire Dragon Real Man smiled, “Whatever you want to give, keep it for yourself! The thirty-six celestial numbers are proof of your connection to the Dao. If even one is missing, it won’t work.”

The old real man pointed to a key acupoint on Chen Ping'an, “A person is a small universe. The celestial number corresponds to the four directions, taking the center of the four corners, which is my heart. The heavenly celestial number, the essence of yin and yang, is the true soil. The virtual and the real are both fundamental teachings of our Dao. Didn’t you refine the five-colored earth into the five elements as your innate item? Just right, you can properly refine these thirty-six blue bricks as the root of that mountain in your heart, which can also nourish the thoughts of the cultivator—killing two birds with one stone. However, refining this item requires consuming a large amount of spiritual energy; shaping the mountain root is no simple task. Later, I’ll teach you a mantra; dragon veins also differ between mountains and waters, and your method of refining items isn’t quite suitable for mountain-making.”

Fire Dragon Real Man picked up a piece of glazed tile, smiling, “Do you know how much this piece of glazed tile would be worth if sold to the right person?”

Chen Ping'an shook his head.

Fire Dragon Real Man extended a palm, shaking it slightly.

Chen Ping'an tentatively asked, “Ten Small Summer coins?”

Fire Dragon Real Man teased, “Ten Small Summer coins? Is it worth my shaking my hand?”

Zhang Shanfeng gently reminded, “Ten Grain Rain coins, Grain Rain coins!”

Chen Ping'an asked, “Would it have to be sold to the Glazed Pavilion in the White Emperor City of Middle Earth?”

Fire Dragon Real Man nodded, “Chatting with an intelligent person is indeed easier. For an ordinary cultivator, a piece of glazed tile is worth at most one Grain Rain coin. For those who don’t know any better, they wouldn’t even want to accept a few Small Summer coins because such items require accumulation to yield remarkable effects; otherwise, they’re just flashy gimmicks and not substantial.”

Chen Ping'an was fortunate he hadn’t sold his possessions at a low price; otherwise, if he were to learn the truth later, his Dao heart would surely be thrown into chaos again.

Fire Dragon Real Man picked a bamboo branch, smiling, “This is one of the ten ancestral bamboos from the Bamboo Sea Cave Heaven’s green mountain god. You could call it a direct descendant. The bamboo is as sturdy as stone, thus able to become a tool, its virtue lies in its toughness. The bamboo stands straight, its joints advancing, humble as a valley, carrying literature and passing it down through generations; all of these are moral qualities. What do you think this particular bamboo you encountered represents? Why do you think you chanced upon it?”

Chen Ping'an shook his head, “I can’t guess.”

Fire Dragon Real Man smiled, “That’s exactly right.”

This was essentially Chen Ping'an’s introspection and subsequent refutation of many certainties.

If the inquiry for truth by a cultivator merely sought a dead heart, then what was the point of so many schools and disciples outside of Daoism? 

Ultimately, it didn’t matter what kind of bamboo one encountered. 

Chen Ping'an actually didn’t know where he stood.

Beside him, Zhang Shanfeng thought his master was right; if that was the case, it would be fine. 

Otherwise, if his master kept making things difficult for Chen Ping'an, it wouldn’t be good.

Fire Dragon Real Man suddenly said, “Shanfeng, go practice your martial arts in the yard.”

Zhang Shanfeng responded with an “oh” and, without asking why, stepped outside.

Fire Dragon Real Man reached out, and the fragments of wooden statues either flew or hovered, gently bumping against each other, swaying, and eventually reassembling into the likeness of a middle-aged Daoist.

It was like the remolding of a mountain and water deity’s golden body.

Looking at this “middle-aged Daoist,” Fire Dragon Real Man sighed gently.

Then he set aside his nostalgic thoughts, his expression serious, and solemnly asked, “Chen Ping'an, where did this deity statue come from?”

Chen Ping'an recounted his experience of visiting the mountain for treasure hunting in general.

He skipped over many details regarding Daoist Sun’s deeds at the immortal estate ruins.

However, Chen Ping'an still underestimated Fire Dragon Real Man’s knowledge and Dao techniques.

Fire Dragon Real Man gazed at the wooden deity statue and slowly said, “This person was killed by Daoist Lao Er while wearing Daoist robes and wielding a celestial sword. Among his direct disciples, there was one named Song Maolu, a prodigy beyond compare, who gathered nearly sixty percent of the Daoist forces outside Baiyu Jing with his own strength. Imagine what it would be like in our Haoran World if someone could contend with half of Confucianism?”

Chen Ping'an couldn’t imagine it.

Fire Dragon Real Man continued revealing the secrets of other realms, at his level, especially with merits to his name, casually calling out the names of sages and wise men, no longer concerned about taboos. He continued, “As for this deity statue, it’s not the kind of ordinary statue worshipped in various small Daoist temples. It’s an important divine seat second only to this sect’s main image, which you can understand as the Yang Spirit of a cultivator. This wood is refined from the ancestral peach trees planted in Xuandu Temple.”

Fire Dragon Real Man smiled, “And the temple master of Xuandu is the senior brother of this figure, continuously listed among the top ten in the entire Qingming World, hailed as the fifth person who cannot be shaken. The lineage of Daoist sword immortals can be said to be supported by this temple master.”

At this point, Fire Dragon Real Man asked, “Can you be sure there are no hidden dangers?”

Chen Ping'an nodded, “I’m certain!”

Fire Dragon Real Man smiled, “What a good fellow, you’ve struck it rich.”

If an ordinary junior dared to speak such words, Fire Dragon Real Man would truly advise them to think twice. 

But since it was Chen Ping'an, he let it pass.

Moreover, since that Daoist Sun, who ascended back to the Qingming World, was willing to leave behind this item, it itself was an acknowledgment of Chen Ping'an.

Fire Dragon Real Man paused for a moment, glanced at Chen Ping'an, and at that moment, it seemed he understood something, vaguely guessing Qi Jingchun’s good intentions, though he wasn’t sure if he was correct.

Fire Dragon Real Man asked straightforwardly, “Do you have the rare materials prepared for refining the five elements innate items?”

Chen Ping'an nodded, “I do.”

Fire Dragon Real Man nodded, “That’s enough, no need to overdo it.”

Chen Ping'an felt a weight lifted off his shoulders. After all, opportunities only come once. It wasn’t like Cui Dongshan, who prepared three portions of five-colored earth, originally intending to pursue a stable outcome—timing, location, and harmony must all align before starting the refinement. This hesitation was also the reason Chen Ping'an had pondered whether to refine this item upon arriving at the Dragon Palace Cave Heaven.

Fire Dragon Real Man watched this young man who liked to think things through, chuckling.

If it were a mountain and forest cultivator, they would have hurriedly refined it as soon as they got their hands on it.

If it were a lineage-based immortal master, their seniors would have helped strategize, perhaps even more than the disciples themselves would care.

Fire Dragon Real Man reminded, “Before refining, calm your mind first.”

He jokingly added, “Do you have any other treasures? Bring them out for a look?”

Chen Ping'an didn’t hold back, taking out item after item from his storage.

Eventually, he even brought out a page of scripture and a Buddhist scripture.

Upon seeing that page of scripture, Fire Dragon Real Man seemed to understand something.

Fire Dragon Real Man helped evaluate the treasures from the mountain, during which he picked up the exquisite round fan, gently shaking it as if dusting it off, and smiling while handing it back to Chen Ping'an, “Take another look.”

Chen Ping'an accepted the fan, still decorated with a lady holding a fan, but upon closer inspection, he noticed that on the small fan in the lady's hand, there was another depiction of the lady holding a fan, and within that image, there was yet another image. Moments later, Chen Ping'an quickly closed his eyes, clenched his fist, and gently pressed it against his forehead.

Fire Dragon Real Man laughed, “Put it away, cherish it well.”

Fire Dragon Real Man tucked the pair of bamboo Dragon King baskets into his sleeve, “They’re too worn out. I’ll help you repair them. This isn’t just a matter of a few divine coins; only by blending water and fire carefully can they be restored without damaging the essence. You’d best not sell these small baskets; if there’s ever a heavy flood on your own mountain, they can be used for the flood dragon. Remember, the Dragon King baskets, besides being used for suppression, are also miniature dragon palaces in the world; when cultivators use them, they serve as weapons, and if flood dragons dwell within, they become natural water residences.”

Chen Ping'an thanked him.

After Chen Ping'an put away all the items, Fire Dragon Real Man seemed to hesitate, wanting to say something but holding back.

Fire Dragon Real Man smiled, “It shouldn’t be personal matters; I understand. You’re curious about the customs of Padi Peak, right?”

Chen Ping'an gritted his teeth, saying, “Old Real Man, I dare to say, can I teach Zhang Shanfeng some profound Dao techniques?”

Fire Dragon Real Man laughed heartily.

If the realm of cultivators is the most tangible divine coin in the world, then the policies of Fire Dragon Real Man’s Padi Peak precisely do not allow any disciple to discuss matters based on their level of achievement.

The reason for this is not something outsiders should know.

But this young man, at least, was not considered an outsider.

So Fire Dragon Real Man teasingly asked, “Isn’t it strange that I intentionally hide things from Shanfeng?”

Chen Ping'an nodded.

Fire Dragon Real Man turned and walked near the sword immortal hanging on the wall, smiling, “I only select disciples based on their character, not their aptitude. Who says a mountain must contend for those so-called geniuses for its foundation? A stable mountain with many conscientious men of the lower five realms, versus a reckless one of the upper five realms—who’s superior?”

Fire Dragon Real Man withdrew his gaze; it was a good sword, but it was also in conflict.

No wonder it’s Chen Ping'an.

Fire Dragon Real Man turned and smiled, “It’s not because I’ve reached this realm that I can say such things. It’s because I’ve always acted this way, steadfast in pursuing the Dao, cultivating strength and heart, that I’ve achieved the realm I have today. Do you understand?”

Chen Ping'an replied, “Of course.”

Fire Dragon Real Man said, “It’s like I’ve planted a large tree on Padi Peak, producing many branches that bloom and bear fruit in different ways, some high, some low, some earlier, some later.

Some are limited by aptitude, with branches and leaves falling, like many older brothers who ascended the mountain for cultivation before Zhang Shanfeng, who couldn’t break through their bottlenecks and passed away. Some disciples are indeed naturally more suited for cultivation, and their years are longer; their Dao techniques are even higher. For instance, the mountains of Tai Xia, Peach Mountain, Zhi Xuan, and Baiyun—these mountains don’t mean the disciples have reached a higher realm.

The level of Dao techniques doesn’t depend on fists but on the heart of the person. However, it is indeed easier to talk about reason when the Dao techniques are high; the same principles would seem more reasonable. Padi Peak has always tried to avoid the spread of such situations. In my eyes, many disciples who have already passed away are no less than the upper five realms of Baiyun’s lineage; their every word and deed remains in my heart.

Regardless of whether one practices on Padi Peak or goes out to establish their own mountain, I will follow their true nature; I will teach different Dao techniques. Some need to be scolded by their master to correct their path and avoid detours, while others need a push from their master to move faster and be bolder. Generally, though, cultivation depends on the individual after the master leads them in.

Zhang Shanfeng is different. I don’t intentionally teach him; ordinary masters would make their disciples aware. But the way I teach Shanfeng is the most natural; he must know it himself, without needing to know more. Is this selfish? It can be, or it may not be. Whether Zhang Shanfeng’s senior brothers see this is up to them. This is the Padi Peak of true cultivation.”

Fire Dragon Real Man laughed, “The way cultivators view realm, treasures, and opportunities is no different from how common folk view money, power, and fortune; fundamentally, there’s a difference. If cultivators wish to be genuine immortals on the mountain, they must have a different perspective, right? Tough fists, long lives, many techniques—does that make one a superior immortal? There are truly a lot of immortals in this world.”

Chen Ping'an carefully pondered the old real man’s words. 

Today’s words and reasoning from the old real man might become the rules that could be directly applied to the Ruined Mountain.

Fire Dragon Real Man said, “Once you gain higher cultivation, and your reputation grows, naturally, you will encounter more and more outsiders pointing fingers at you, trying to teach you how to be Chen Ping'an.”

The old real man smiled, “So you must remember, people today speak of the ancients, the living speak of the dead; it’s merely bullying the other side for not opening their mouth. Therefore, first, Chen Ping'an, don’t die. Furthermore, the true villains of this world actually love the existence of good people. Only fools continuously despise good people, complaining day and night that they haven’t done enough good deeds. These people can’t understand, can’t be taught, can’t change; their heads are filled with mush, and they’re full of resentment. In my view, they are the most formidable figures in this world, and I can’t do anything about them. 

People talk reason for many reasons, merely to argue for winning and losing, to feel good, thus preferring extremes. They fear that if they don’t do this, their reasoning won’t be sufficient or grand enough. Such people seem full of reasoning; in fact, they are the least reasonable. You must be careful of these clever ones. That’s why I genuinely admire the Confucian sage. When talking reason, right is right, good is good; reasoning isn’t fighting. It isn’t winning by knocking the other person down and forcing them to plead for mercy. It’s about connecting reason, benefiting each other in the end.”

Although Chen Ping'an had remained silent throughout, Fire Dragon Real Man already knew part of the answer to a certain conjecture.

That was enough.

What a long and profound intention spanning thousands of years.

It turned out one could also protect the Dao like this.

It seemed he had underestimated Qi Jingchun’s knowledge earlier.

Surely the lineage of the Confucian sage, each of them was fiercely protective of their own.

Thus, Fire Dragon Real Man said a profoundly meaningful phrase, “Chen Ping'an, sometimes, what you think you have completely lost is what you truly hold onto. Therefore, some disappointments you think are actually where others find hope.”

Finally, the old real man patted the young man’s shoulder, “Alright, seize the moment and refine your third innate item quickly! This treatment of me personally guarding your refinement, ordinary cultivators wouldn’t even dare to dream of it. Otherwise, how would a third realm Qi practitioner have the audacity to wander around?”

Chen Ping'an smiled wryly, “But you just said you don’t judge cultivators based on their realm.”

Fire Dragon Real Man laughed, “You, Chen Ping'an, are not a Padi Peak cultivator.”

Chen Ping'an helplessly said, “That’s reasonable.”

The old real man clicked his tongue, “You really aren’t good at flattery.”

Chen Ping'an nodded, “I’m not good at speaking.”

Fire Dragon Real Man chuckled, “Being a scoundrel is also a way of being a good person without regrets.”

With Fire Dragon Real Man around, it would be hard for anything to happen on Fushui Island.

Chen Ping'an was currently in seclusion refining his third innate item.

Before this, Fire Dragon Real Man first taught him an ancient refining mantra named “Refining the Three Mountains,” allowing Chen Ping'an to refine the Daoist essence of those thirty-six blue bricks, solidifying the mountain shrine as the root vein of a mountain. In the end, this young man actually asked whether he could refine just the essence without refining the blue bricks themselves. Fire Dragon Real Man didn’t question further about what use the thirty-six blue bricks would have without their Daoist essence and water essence, simply saying he could.

Otherwise, once the wooden innate item was successfully refined, the spiritual aura would be immense; the movements from the water palace would be manageable, but since the mountain shrine was crafted from the five-colored earth of Baoping Continent, it would inevitably influence the spiritual aura. If the balance among the three items was lost from the start, without care, it would require Chen Ping'an to spend a lot of time, materials, and finances on repairs—Fire Dragon Real Man couldn’t afford to lose face over that.

Fire Dragon Real Man was truly a person at the peak of the mountain, observing Chen Ping'an’s current realm and situation with clarity.

In the water palace, whether it was the innate item of the water character seal or the wall painting that hadn’t yet been completed but already had a semblance of form, along with that small pond, there was no need to demand more.

Among the sons of heaven of the North Julu Continent, those with such a water palace formation were few and far between; moreover, it was crucial to look ahead to when Chen Ping'an could turn that pond into a deep well and eventually into a dragon pool.

As for Chen Ping'an’s innate mountain shrine, its material was relatively ordinary, yet it was no less than the ancestral hall of the sect. However, it excelled in longevity. Regardless, it could not compare to the water palace and the future wooden residence.

However, Chen Ping'an refining the Daoist essence of those thirty-six blue bricks and separating the water essence actually consumed a whole ten days.

If it had been one of his fellow disciples who opened their own mountains, three days would have sufficed.

Fire Dragon Real Man didn’t think it was a big deal; on the path of the Dao, some people walk quickly because they started early, but climbing mountains is more challenging at later stages. It’s inevitable to slow down as one progresses, which is why only those who burst through their limits at the beginning are considered geniuses. Those who reach the Earth Immortal stage don’t continue to charge forward as they did before. Even Li Liu is no exception; everyone will linger for a time at the Nascent Soul stage before slowing down after reaching the upper five realms.

However, there are a few, an extremely small number, who grow faster as they continue walking.

The former are the typical sons of heaven, the latter can make those sons of heaven happy for many years, only to suddenly find out they’re also ordinary.

Chen Ping'an was busy cultivating.

Zhang Shanfeng lounged around on Fushui Island, refining his Qi, practicing martial arts, and chatting with his master.

One rainy day, Zhang Shanfeng held his umbrella and strolled along the shore, encountering a boy poking his head out of the water, who asked him a perplexing question about whether he would cry and run back to tell his master if he punched him.

Zhang Shanfeng squatted by the water, inquiring about the punch’s weight.

That boy was also bored and began discussing the punch’s intensity with the young Daoist.

After their conversation, Water Justice Li Yuan felt hopeful.

In the end, however, the young Daoist directly said, “I think it’s better to ask my master first before deciding whether to take that punch.”

Li Yuan felt as if struck by a bolt from the blue; for the past few days, he had secretly observed this person, thinking that this little Daoist seemed quite silly. How could he be so unassuming?

Zhang Shanfeng couldn’t help but laugh, “I’m just joking with you. I’ve wandered around Fushui Island many times; it’s rare to chat with someone.”

Li Yuan, who had only shown his head, leaped out of the water, sitting cross-legged, hands on his knees, and asked, “Little Daoist, why do you have such a master, and yet your realm is still so lacking?”

Zhang Shanfeng smiled, “My master can’t replace his disciples in cultivation.”

He actually felt that this boy before him seemed to have some issues with his head.

Li Yuan shook his head, feeling pity for the little fool from Padi Peak, clicking his tongue, “Little Daoist, you really don’t know how to appreciate your luck. Your aptitude must not be great either; if it were someone else, they would have swiftly reached the Golden Core and Nascent Soul realms. Then they would cry and ask their master for some heavy treasures to carry with them, and every time they descended the mountain, wouldn’t they walk with everyone calling them ‘Grandpa’?”

Zhang Shanfeng smiled, “But it’s not that I’m a little Daoist from Padi Peak, just boasting here. With your temperament, you wouldn’t be able to become a Daoist from Padi Peak. However, everyone has their own fateful path. Just because you can’t become a Daoist from Padi Peak doesn’t mean it’s a bad thing. I think you must be some water god from the Dragon Palace Cave Heaven, right? I’m quite envious of you; you were born with that water-dividing divine ability. I can’t do that; I can only follow my master to learn immortal techniques on the mountain, and I learn slower than each one.”

Li Yuan squinted with a sneer, “But I see you, little Daoist, don’t seem to be anxious at all?”

Zhang Shanfeng rolled his eyes, “If being anxious works, do you see me anxious? I know being anxious doesn’t help, so why bother?”

Li Yuan sighed, “Your old real man has taken on such a mundane disciple; he must be heartbroken.”

Zhang Shanfeng chuckled.

Li Yuan became more convinced that this guy was indeed a little fool.

Then Fire Dragon Real Man must be an old fool too?

Thinking of this, Li Yuan felt a bit relieved and laughed along with the young Daoist.

But soon, Li Yuan found himself unable to laugh anymore.

Fire Dragon Real Man stood beside Zhang Shanfeng, smiling.

Li Yuan stood up and said, “Congratulations, old real man, for taking on such an astonishing disciple. He’s not just one in ten thousand; the Dao is promising, indeed promising!”

This was likely what made Li Yuan more impressive than the sect master of the Water Dragon Sect, Sun Jie. 

Sun Jie, along with the Lord of Shenzhao and his colleague Shen Lin, who had the guts to say such things in front of Fire Dragon Real Man?

Fire Dragon Real Man said, “Go inform the islands of Baijia and Cangyan, and then greet the South Xun Water Palace. No matter what happens next, don’t be nervous.”

Since it was a serious matter.

As the Water Justice, Li Yuan stopped being playful, nodded, and transformed into streaks of golden light, disappearing. He didn’t want to show his face at Baijia and Cangyan Islands, so it would be simpler to let Shen Lin and the South Xun Water Palace clean up the mess.

As long as it didn’t involve the Jidu Temple and the incense of the cave heaven, Li Yuan couldn’t be bothered to meddle.

Zhang Shanfeng noticed that it had stopped raining on Fushui Island, so he put away his oiled paper umbrella and quietly said, “Master, I feel there’s something odd about Fushui Island; this rain comes and goes without any sign.”

Fire Dragon Real Man nodded, “Shanfeng, you’re quite observant and perceptive.”

Zhang Shanfeng smiled, “I learned it from Chen Ping'an.”

Fire Dragon Real Man asked with a smile, “Then what has Chen Ping'an learned from you?”

Zhang Shanfeng thought carefully, “Crying poor and hungry?”

Fire Dragon Real Man chuckled, “That’s not bad.”

Approximately a stick of incense later.

Zhang Shanfeng and Fire Dragon Real Man boarded the talisman boat leased from the Water Dragon Sect, heading toward the sea of clouds, looking down at Fushui Island from afar.

Zhang Shanfeng suddenly noticed a carriage leaping out from between the islands of Baijia and Cangyan, with a goddess standing in front, seemingly using divine power to harness the spiritual energy of heaven and earth, gathering it towards Fushui Island.

Zhang Shanfeng suddenly remarked, “If Chen Ping'an learns of this water goddess’s actions later, he’ll probably be grateful for a long time.”

Fire Dragon Real Man slowly said, “Heaven and earth give birth to all things to nurture humans; how one views heaven and earth is the great scholarship of a cultivator. It’s the same table of food; some people gorge themselves, some chew slowly, some express thanks and gratitude—that’s the good-hearted; some settle accounts and worry about owing even a copper coin—that’s us cultivators. Some people flip the table after eating, fearing others can also feast; those behind will call out for the strong, filled with reverence, and seek food elsewhere, imitating this behavior. They won’t overturn the table but will put down their chopsticks and curse before leaving, perhaps even spitting in the bowls and dishes on their way out. 

Some people, after standing up, tidy up the bowls and dishes, unwilling to leave immediately, helping to stabilize the shaky table and chairs. Those waiting to eat will complain and might even kick that person.”

Zhang Shanfeng felt a bit confused.

Fire Dragon Real Man sighed, “What disappoints Confucian sages the most is always the scholars. What tarnishes Daoist teachings are cultivators. What corrupts Buddhist teachings is always those who merely chant scriptures.”

Zhang Shanfeng asked, “What should we do?”

The old real man slowly said, “Restrain oneself. Seek truth. Self-liberation.”

Zhang Shanfeng, full of worry, softly asked, “How is Chen Ping'an doing?”

Fire Dragon Real Man considered for a moment, “Qi Jingchun’s teachings have never fallen to the ground.”

Zhang Shanfeng asked again, “Does Chen Ping'an know?”

Fire Dragon Real Man shook his head, “He has never known.”

Zhang Shanfeng suddenly said, “I think this is how it should be.”

Fire Dragon Real Man was taken aback for a moment, focusing his gaze, shaking his head and laughing, “What a quaint wooden house in a small alley, seemingly appearing out of nowhere with a locust tree door. This is a bit unreasonable!”

The locust tree door was slightly ajar, and as one passed by, they seemed to hear faint cries.

Inside stood a peach tree, without any leaves or flowers.

Unbeknownst to when, those soft sobs, like a gentle knock on the heart, would gradually dissipate, and no one knew when the peach leaves and blossoms would meet.

It could be next spring.

Or it might take longer.

Outside the small alley stood a solitary young man in a blue robe, staring intently towards the not-so-distant alley, where a gleeful child was bouncing home, exclaiming that he would soon be able to eat candied hawthorns.

The Chen Ping'an who was no longer a child slowly reached out his hand as if greeting that child.

That carefree, innocent child paused, tilting his head to gaze at the adult.

In the end, it seemed the child didn’t recognize who the adult was.

Yet the child’s laughter faded, and without a sound, he quietly walked past the adult, entering the house and closing the half-open courtyard door.

Leaving only an adult self standing outside the door.

Eventually, that child seemed to grow a little, taller than before, becoming much darker. The child opened the door, stepping out of the house, carrying a large basket, filled with pots and bowls, a ceramic jar for boiling medicine, and tattered, faded spring couplets.

The child lowered his head, gripping the rope tightly that held the basket, swaying as he left the house and the alley, never to return home.

**(End of Chapter)**

 ### Chapter 656: Reunion at the Estuary

The activity on Waterfowl Island (Fushui Dao) was quite intense.

It required the Water God, Shen Lin, to personally navigate the waters to reach Waterfowl Island. Fortunately, the cultivators from the White Armor (Bai Jia) and Azure Beard (Cang Ran) islands had received prior notice from the Southern Breath Water Palace (Nanxun Shuidian), informing them that a certain wild and free expert on Waterfowl Island was about to break through a vital barrier.

Two trusted attendants of the Water Goddess, one a lamp-lighting official from the Southern Breath Water Palace and the other a water vein examiner, were each staying as guests on the White Armor and Azure Beard islands. This was not only a matter of respect but also a form of "military oversight."

On the clouds above the sea, Zhang Shanfeng asked, “Master, how long has it been? Chen Ping'an has clearly succeeded in refining his life-bound object, so why hasn’t he come back to his senses yet?”

Real Master Huo Long replied, “It’s that simple to shut oneself away and think. Smart people who get stuck in a rut find it hard to get out. They either have to retrace their steps step by step or break through it forcefully, creating a new path.”

Li Yuan sat cross-legged at a distance, resting his chin on his hands, breathing in and out like a fish blowing bubbles. Even the revered Water Rites Master had become so bored that he had no one left to talk to.

Real Master Huo Long turned to Li Yuan and asked, “Old Li, still playing? Do you know what you’ve missed?”

Li Yuan replied, “I haven’t missed this excitement at all; I’ve been watching with my eyes wide open from start to finish.”

Real Master Huo Long chuckled, “It’s fortunate that the divine spirits don’t have such guts.”

Li Yuan rolled his eyes, “What, regret?”

Real Master Huo Long inquired, “Want me to sell you a bottle of regret medicine? Once this village is gone, there won’t be any more shops. You’d better think it over.”

Li Yuan’s eyes darted around; he figured this old fellow wasn’t just toying with him out of boredom. So he asked, “What’s the price?”

Real Master Huo Long laughed, “A bottle of top-quality Water Rites Pills, not the kind used to fool river gods.”

Li Yuan grinned and shook his head, “No thanks. Old Master, I really can’t take out a bottle of my life-bound pills. After all, even if I don’t manage things anymore, I still have to hand over one water pill to the Water Dragon Sect every ten years.”

This decade he would give one to Sun Jie, and next decade, one to Shao Jingzhi. The Northern and Southern sects would take turns receiving them. As for what was done with the water pill afterward—whether it was used as a favor to some shrewd guest or kept for himself to reward the direct disciples of the Patriarch Hall—Li Yuan wouldn’t pry.

Real Master Huo Long wasn’t talking about just one or two Water Rites Pills, but an entire bottle filled with rich incense and vital essence, at least nine pills.

If it were three to five hundred years ago, Li Yuan might have considered it.

But now, in his current pitiful state, he was no better off than Shen Lin, whose golden body was on the verge of collapse. The Southern Breath Water Palace was so shamelessly trying to add luster to Waterfowl Island. Was it really due to Shen Lin’s magnanimity? This woman was frugal and prudent; it was more likely she thought she had grasped a lifeline, treating Real Master Huo Long as a living bodhisattva to save her from disaster. It was all a matter of breaking something that was already broken.

Li Yuan shook his head, thinking to himself that when people speak of the mercilessness of the Great Dao, they are not just talking about the mountains but also about the heavens.

And that “Li Liu” was one of the few existences in the heavens.

To put it frankly, Shen Lin’s commotion would cost her several decades of time. Had she forgotten Real Master Huo Long’s original words? The Southern Breath Water Palace could simply watch from the sidelines.

Zhang Shanfeng looked puzzled.

Real Master Huo Long smiled and said, “Forcing a cow to drink water is hard.”

Zhang Shanfeng softly asked, “Has Chen Ping'an broken through?”

Real Master Huo Long shook his head, “Still at the third realm, but he’s at a bottleneck. For Chen Ping'an, his willow tendon realm can be considered a genuine ‘stay’ realm. There’s no way around it; he has faced the three major difficulties of breaking the heart demon, merging the Dao, and seeking truth early on, and with the Long Life Bridge now broken, it’s only right that he stumbles along. Otherwise, I’d have to suspect this kid is the reincarnation of some mountain-top figure.”

Zhang Shanfeng asked, “Isn’t it good to be a reincarnation of a celestial being after leaving the world? I’ve heard that many ancestral masters of sects leave a path back for themselves before closing the life-death barrier, seeking their reincarnated selves and paving the way for the continuation of their sect’s incense.”

Real Master Huo Long shook his head, “Not good. I am not my past self. If one can’t recall previous lives, that’s somewhat acceptable, but if they remember some things but not all, that’s a big problem.”

Of course, the natural-born Li Liu was an exception; for her, it was just a change of skin, effectively meaning she had never died.

Sleeping every night was merely a nap; it was death that was a deep sleep.

If a cultivator only seeks to evade death and forcibly seizes the heavenly secrets, it would be akin to sneaky thieves moving at night, reincarnating without their original soul, piecing together a person from fragments. In the end, who is who in that half-alive state?

However, Real Master Huo Long could understand some of the fears of the higher realm cultivators, even if he didn’t fully approve.

Some demonic sects that like to take alternative paths would even light a stick of life incense for their cultivators. Historically, many cultivators who merely stared at that stick of incense for a moment would have their Dao hearts collapse, completely falling into madness. This was simply a case of scaring oneself to death.

Real Master Huo Long seldom comforted his disciple’s thoughts and smiled, “Earlier, when I said Chen Ping'an was limping along, it was more about the muddled path of his heart, which has affected his true nature. In fact, a temporary low realm is not a big deal.”

Zhang Shanfeng remained worried, “Chen Ping'an owes so much debt; what should he do? This guy fears owing favors and money the most.”

Real Master Huo Long laughed, “Some big worries, Chen Ping'an actually doesn’t fear. For example, on the road to climbing a mountain, if he’s focused on walking slowly but discovers he can bend down to pick up money just a few steps ahead, even if it’s just a snowflake of money, do you think Chen Ping'an would walk faster? Each time he picks up a piece of money, a burden is lifted, and over time, he’ll naturally walk faster.”

Zhang Shanfeng suddenly understood; his master was really sharp, having seen Chen Ping'an just twice and understanding him so well.

Real Master Huo Long suddenly said, “With everything settled, we can return to Waterfowl Island now.”

Li Yuan finally couldn’t hold back and asked, “What realm is this Mr. Chen exactly?”

Real Master Huo Long and his disciple’s conversation was lost on Li Yuan.

The foremost fire law cultivator in the world. As for water law, he should be firmly within the top ten.

Let’s not forget that Real Master Huo Long was also the external Grand Master of Longhu Mountain. What kind of place was the Longhu Mountain Grand Master’s residence? The mountain cultivators have always revered worldly techniques, especially thunder law, as the most supreme. The heavenly pivot governs all laws. The Grand Master’s five thunder orthodox method of “creation lies in my hands” is the legitimate doctrine of thunder law throughout the world. Can Real Master Huo Long’s thunder law be weak?

Generally speaking, the various external Grand Masters of Longhu Mountain can study all forms of Longhu Mountain techniques except for the Grand Master seal and the immortal sword.

Thus, Real Master Huo Long could stand out in the sword-fighting-laden North Julu Continent, remaining so ethereal and unique.

Ignoring Li Yuan, Real Master Huo Long descended from the clouds with Zhang Shanfeng, arriving at the residence on Waterfowl Island.

Chen Ping'an had already exited his seclusion, his divine aura restrained and his skin glowing. However, having just refined his life-bound object, he had yet to stabilize his energy field, causing the spiritual energy within him to fluctuate, making him appear even more ethereal and detached. Once the wooden residence settled, this minor celestial quality would be easily controlled.

Real Master Huo Long nodded in appreciation, “When I was at the fifth realm, I didn’t have this kind of bearing.”

Chen Ping'an clasped his fists in thanks.

Real Master Huo Long didn’t mind Chen Ping'an's formalities this time; in the cultivation path, when guarding a barrier for someone in seclusion who successfully emerges, some surface formality is still required.

Real Master Huo Long said, “Since you’ve succeeded, my Dao and Shanfeng won’t linger much longer; there are still a lot of matters to attend to at the Flat Earth Peak.”

Zhang Shanfeng muttered, “Isn’t sleeping anywhere the same as sleeping?”

Real Master Huo Long wasn’t the least bit annoyed by his disciple’s mockery; instead, he laughed and explained, “Of course, it’s more comfortable to take a nap in your own grass hut.”

Cultivators occupy the world's famous mountains and rivers to distance themselves from mundane affairs for good reason. Immortals move into the mountains. The world is filled with troubles, and it’s hard to let go of attachments. Therefore, it is best to enter the famous mountains, as it purifies the body and mind.

Zhang Shanfeng nodded, “I do miss those senior brothers and nephews.”

Chen Ping'an said, “I might trouble the old master with one more thing.”

Zhang Shanfeng quickly replied, “Not troublesome at all.”

Real Master Huo Long smiled but said nothing.

Zhang Shanfeng was afraid his master would think he was being selfish, so he quickly said, “Master, Chen Ping'an knows his limits. If he says it’s troublesome, it shouldn’t be too much trouble. This is like us getting a favor for free. Before he returns to the Bottle of Treasure Continent, he’ll definitely come to visit our family. When the time comes, I’ll show him around, especially places like Peach Mountain and the vicinity of Tai Xia Peak, which I haven’t visited much. That’s just not right.”

Real Master Huo Long nodded, smiling at Chen Ping'an, “Go ahead.”

Chen Ping'an then expressed that he hoped to keep one of the 122 green glazed tiles for himself, while the rest could be sold in the City of the White Emperor in the Central Continent, for a total of six hundred Gu Yu coins.

Zhang Shanfeng was dumbfounded, about to speak, but was stopped by Chen Ping'an’s glance.

Real Master Huo Long seemed to weigh the pros and cons, smiling but saying nothing.

Chen Ping'an quietly waited for a response.

Distant water cannot quench immediate thirst.

The current situation on Ruined Mountain desperately needed divine coins; there were holes everywhere that needed filling, and none were small. 

Upgrading the Lotus Root Blessed Land to a middle blessed land was one thing, but it was of utmost importance. If not counting the proceeds from Wei Ban's third Mountain Water Spirit Night Feast, if he could sell that pile of glazed tiles, he could immediately earn six hundred Gu Yu coins, enough to close all the gaps and perhaps even have a surplus of about two hundred Gu Yu coins. He would send half of this surplus to Zhu Lian as savings for Ruined Mountain, to avoid being caught in a bind with every expense. 

As for the favors owed, since there was no choice, it was better to owe a great deal but ensure it was infrequent. This was far better than having to owe smaller favors to many people, which could never be returned, thus negating the essence of mutual aid and leaving friends feeling they had met with bad luck. In the end, the kindness in this world always requires a give and take.

Moreover, how could he continue to take advantage of Wei Ban? A dignified divine spirit of the Northern Sacred Mountain—was it appropriate to sweep the ground in his jurisdiction? After all, Chen Ping'an was a burden-carrying monk. Even if he had to run far with a well, wasn’t that something?

Chen Ping'an could keep a hundred Gu Yu coins for himself to purchase two or three imitation swords from the Sword Immortal Mountain. If the price were right, much lower than expected, perhaps he could buy a few more and give them as gifts.

Additionally, the construction and operation of the mountain protection formation on Ruined Mountain would be another considerable expense.

Including Gray Mist Mountain and Ao Bei Mountain, the selection and placement of the numerous new mountain peaks were third on the list. In fact, Jiang Shangzhen had initially come up with a pretext to thank Chen Ping'an for helping the True Realm Sect gain an additional Sword Immortal for their absent attendance at Wei Ban's two Night Feasts, but they already had three significant treasures. The Dragon King’s basket that Real Master Huo Long took for repairs also counted among them; the rest would need Ruined Mountain to continue financing.

Thus, Chen Ping'an could only keep two green glazed tiles for himself as a token. After all, this item was hard to come by, and keeping it on Ruined Mountain would serve as a good omen for double blessings.

Real Master Huo Long laughed, “Six hundred coins? At half price? Chen Ping'an, you’re making a bad deal.”

Chen Ping'an smiled and replied, “It depends on the person. If it were some wealthy merchant, I’d sell it to him for two thousand coins without batting an eye.”

According to Real Master Huo Long’s earlier appraisal, one hundred and twenty glazed tiles could fetch twelve hundred Gu Yu coins at the Glazed Pavilion in the City of the White Emperor.

However, some calculations aren’t that simple.

Accidentally picking up such a large pile of glazed tiles was a stroke of immense fortune. Otherwise, based on Chen Ping'an's own thoughts, factoring in Old Master Huan Yun's uncertainty about the price of the tiles, he would probably be overjoyed to sell each tile for a small summer coin, and he might even end up leaving behind the last two tiles.

Selling it at Flat Earth Peak for half price.

Such a choice would not only allow him to immediately obtain an unimaginably large amount of Gu Yu coins, but it would also serve as a token of gratitude for Real Master Huo Long’s guidance and protection. Furthermore, it would spare him the trouble of dealing with potential mishaps in trading with the Central Continent’s City of the White Emperor. Ultimately, Chen Ping'an hoped that before returning south, he could visit Flat Earth Peak and seek out Zhang Shanfeng, giving him a bit of confidence instead of being heavily indebted to the old master for a significant favor while still shamelessly mooching off his food and drink.

This plan contained both calculation and spontaneity.

Good intentions lay within, alongside numerous private thoughts, allowing Chen Ping'an to act openly without concern.

Real Master Huo Long said, “Hurry up and refine the scattered and chaotic spiritual energy within the three critical energy fields; otherwise, it will have to be returned to Waterfowl Island and Dragon Palace Cave, wasting Li Yuan and Shen Lin’s good intentions. It’s like when a host kindly offers a cup of tea, and the guest only takes a few sips before leaving—what’s that all about? That’s the first point.”

“Second, human efforts are limited. It’s impossible to gather all the spiritual energy; it’s unavoidable. After all, he’s just a third realm qi refining cultivator. You can’t truly drink tea to the point of bursting; the host sincerely entertains the guest and doesn’t wish to help the guest collect their corpse afterward; doesn’t that bring bad luck? So you should study the alchemical formulas for refining mountains and rivers and continue refining the Dao intent within the Daoist bricks; this is also a part of cultivation. Before this, you were in a treasure mountain but didn’t know it. These high-level alchemical formulas aren’t just for refining objects. Spend more time pondering them yourself.”

“The third point is the one hundred twenty glazed tiles. Six hundred Gu Yu coins is the price you set yourself; no buyer in the world will raise the price on their own. The impoverished Daoist is indeed famous for being broke in the North Julu Continent. Luckily, it shouldn’t be difficult to borrow a few hundred Gu Yu coins from disciples like Peach Mountain and Zhi Xuan.”

At this point, Real Master Huo Long smiled, “Rest assured, not a single Gu Yu coin will be shorted to you.”

Chen Ping'an once again bowed in thanks.

Zhang Shanfeng felt conflicted.

He was torn between realizing his master and senior brothers were so wealthy and that Chen Ping'an must be suffering a loss, which amounted to six hundred Gu Yu coins. Chen Ping'an wasn’t upset, but Zhang Shanfeng felt a pang in his heart. After all, their sect had earned six hundred Gu Yu coins. Isn’t this what people call “the fat water doesn’t flow to outsiders’ fields”?

So no matter what he said now—whether happy or not—it would seem suspicious.

Zhang Shanfeng felt a bit uncomfortable.

Life is hard.

Real Master Huo Long suddenly asked, “Chen Ping'an, what do you think of Zhang Shanfeng’s fist technique?”

Chen Ping'an was taken aback and honestly replied, “It’s a bit slow, not yet complete.”

Zhang Shanfeng felt embarrassed, nearly wanting to dig a hole to bury himself. Master, you don’t think Chen Ping'an’s talent is too good and are trying to inflate your disciple’s ego to save some face, do you? There’s no need for that.

He knew his own capabilities; Zhang Shanfeng had a good grasp of his own weight. No matter what he learned, it was all half-baked. Going down the mountain to travel and slay demons, he was still far from adequate. Therefore, Zhang Shanfeng had firmly decided to only descend the mountain once he could genuinely claim to have achieved some mastery in Dao techniques.

Furthermore, Zhi Xuan was the one with good talent. The little disciples from Flat Earth Peak loved to speculate on whether this Master Uncle Yuan was an immortal at the Golden Core level.

Real Master Huo Long said, “Chen Ping'an, your path into martial arts was indeed not a mistake.”

Chen Ping'an smiled, “Actually, it wasn’t my choice. Initially, there was no choice; if I didn’t rely on practicing martial arts to survive, I wouldn’t have made it far.”

Real Master Huo Long nodded, “No matter what, treating yourself well is the first step to treating others well. You must be clear about this. Afterward, when giving this world good deeds, ask yourself what your heart needs. For me, I feel it’s not really necessary.”

Chen Ping'an pondered for a moment and smiled, “Understood.”

Real Master Huo Long remembered something and smiled, “Since you enjoy thinking so much and walking around Waterfowl Island, and you can even articulate ‘not yet complete,’ I’ll share a little story with you. After hearing it, whatever you think is what it is. There was a scholar who crossed a river with a boatman. The scholar, well-versed in literature, preached many great principles, making the boatman, who couldn’t read, blush with shame. Suddenly, a great wave overturned the boat, and both fell into the water. The drowning scholar could only rely on the boatman’s one skill, contemplating whether to save him or not.”

Chen Ping'an said, “I’ll remember that; I’ll think more about its deeper meaning.”

Real Master Huo Long seemed to smile and said slowly, “Is there really a need for deeper meaning? Just because I’m a Daoist with a certain status, you feel compelled to listen and think carefully.”

Chen Ping'an was about to say something.

Real Master Huo Long waved his hand, “I’m just a person on the shore; I don’t need to listen to the boatman’s answer.”

Finally, Real Master Huo Long waved his large sleeve, casually collecting the green glazed tiles into his robe. 

It is said that cultivators on the mountain can hold vast amounts in their sleeves.

Chen Ping'an felt a bit envious. With such mountain-level divine powers, being a burden-carrying monk would feel so natural.

Real Master Huo Long led the way to the bank, and the talisman boat quietly hovered at the ferry, floating with the water’s rise and fall.

Zhang Shanfeng and Chen Ping'an slowed their pace, walking side by side.

Chen Ping'an said, “I can only perceive a bit of meaning in your fist technique. After you reach Flat Earth Peak, make sure you don’t neglect practicing this fist technique alongside your other studies.”

Zhang Shanfeng asked with a smile, “Then do I count as your half-fist technique master?”

Chen Ping'an gave a single word: “Scram.”

Zhang Shanfeng softly said, “Don’t worry; I’ll urge Master Yuan from Zhi Xuan Peak to hurry over to Dragon Palace Cave. Although he’s skilled in Dao, his temperament is quite good.”

In front, Real Master Huo Long chuckled.

As for the disciple Yuan Lingdian, it was hard to say whether his temperament was good or not. In the past, this kid had been the most unruly, having earned his realm through sheer effort, but later he was confined by his master in the Peach Mountain stone cave for ten years. After emerging, he was then grounded for sixty years, which had significantly improved his character.

Chen Ping'an stood at the ferry, watching the talisman boat ascend into the sea of clouds.

He planned to take the initiative to visit the Southern Breath Water Palace to thank the Water Goddess. However, how to go would need to be first discussed with Li Yuan.

Li Yuan waited anxiously, and once the talisman boat finally left, he immediately appeared on Waterfowl Island.

Without Real Master Huo Long’s presence in Dragon Palace Cave, everything looked friendlier and more approachable.

Upon hearing that Chen Ping'an wished to go to the Southern Breath Water Palace, Li Yuan said it would be simple. He employed water law divine powers to take Chen Ping'an on a distant water journey.

He wasn’t petty enough to disallow this Mr. Chen from establishing a good relationship with Shen Lin.

Shen Lin had diligently maintained the operation of the Water Palace summer retreat for so many years; Li Yuan just acknowledged that he had been slightly lazy. Besides, they each had their own duties and wouldn’t overstep. In fact, Li Yuan’s intentional or unintentional “failure to be sociable” and his deliberate distance from the Water Dragon Sect’s leader, Sun Jie, had made the private friendship between the Southern Breath Water Palace and the Southern Sect’s Shao Jingzhi exceptionally precious, allowing Shao Jingzhi to feel grateful, even though she had entered the Jade Purity realm. Facing the Water Goddess Shen Lin, who was merely at the Nascent Soul realm, she still maintained a respectful demeanor as a junior.

Upon arriving at the summer retreat, they entered through the side door without obstruction.

Being the Water Rites Master still held considerable weight.

Moreover, the ladies of the Southern Breath Water Palace were familiar with Li Yuan, viewing him as a member of their own. 

Additionally, in this strictly regulated Southern Breath Water Palace, Li Yuan’s slightly risqué jokes were even more popular. Many qualified attendants and palace maids enjoyed listening to this seemingly youthful Water Rites Master recount tales of talented men and beautiful women from the mortal realm. When he struck the right chord, they would burst into laughter, and those with a bit of shyness would leave with a blush, murmuring a playful “disgusting” as they sauntered off, their slender waists swaying enticingly.

Walking in the familiar Water Palace, Li Yuan couldn’t help but lament that if he still had an unblemished golden body, he would truly be living the life of an immortal.

Shen Lin quickly came out to personally greet the two.

Li Yuan initially hadn’t intended to get involved; having led Chen Ping'an to meet Shen Lin would be a job well done, and he intended to find some of the ladies to chat, asking if they had taken a liking to any young talents from the Water Dragon Sect and whether he needed to play matchmaker to create some subtle encounters or misunderstandings. But that Mr. Chen, however, said he would only sit for a while before returning to Waterfowl Island. So, Li Yuan had to feel a bit guilty, putting aside those embarrassing stories he had recently heard for now. Over the past few centuries, he had told countless embellished tales about the mountains and valleys, yet it seemed the most popular ones were always about Jiang Shangzhen’s romantic escapades. It really was a matter of no justice in the world.

Chen Ping'an held a small tea cake made from Xuanbi tea in his hand; the gift was light, and the sentiment not heavy. It could only be described as humble.

There was no way; this visit, Chen Ping'an truly hadn’t prepared any suitable gift to show his gratitude.

However, Shen Lin was very happy, showing no signs of pretense. Upon hearing it was from the Cai Que Mansion’s Xuanbi, she even insisted on keeping Chen Ping'an and Li Yuan to brew tea in the pavilion beside the flower garden, telling Chen Gongzi not to mind, saying she would serve the gift to her guests.

This time, Shen Lin didn’t reveal her true appearance but instead used magic to conceal her scarred face.

As Chen Ping'an enjoyed the tea, he couldn’t help but feel emotional. This being was clearly a mountain and water spirit yet knew how to interact with people so well.

Shen Lin also had her own thoughts. This young cultivator, able to have Real Master Huo Long personally guarding him, just from his demeanor while drinking tea, suggested he surely came from a sect with a notable lineage or a family of wealth.

Chen Ping'an asked about the methods of refining water pills and how to reduce waste.

Shen Lin naturally wouldn’t hide any secrets, explaining many critical points, allowing Chen Ping'an to gain a lot. This was the difference made by having a wise mentor on the cultivation path.

Perhaps wild cultivators could also seize many opportunities from the immortal sect’s teachings, but the key to successfully utilizing those opportunities and treasures lay in the orderly inheritance and continuous lineage of the immortal family. Many subtle discrepancies, accumulated over time, could lead directly to discrepancies in realms, especially the significant difference between the Dragon Gate and Golden Core realms.

Throughout the conversation, Shen Lin didn’t ask a single question about Chen Ping'an's background, not even testing him.

After finishing the tea, Chen Ping'an took his leave and hurried back to Waterfowl Island.

It was still Li Yuan who personally escorted him.

Upon arriving at the residence on Waterfowl Island, Chen Ping'an sat on a mat and began to plan his next steps in cultivation.

Li Yuan returned to the Southern Breath Water Palace, where he bumped into Shen Lin, who hadn’t even tidied up the tea set in the pavilion.

Li Yuan actually didn’t enjoy drinking tea. However, since Shen Lin had brewed it again, he didn’t mind and leisurely sipped the tea. It was better than plain water, right?

After Real Master Huo Long’s arrival and departure, Shen Lin seemed to feel much lighter in mood.

The two chatted about some recent events on the North Julu Continent.

For instance, Ji Yue and Gu You had both perished together, Liu Jinglong from the Taihui Sword Sect had begun seclusion, and the female head of the Qingliang Sect had surprisingly found a Dao partner.

When Li Yuan mentioned that Sect Master He, Shen Lin, couldn’t help but pound her chest and exclaim how such a divine beauty should never fall into the hands of filthy men.

Shen Lin looked at Li Yuan, her expression a bit dazed.

She somewhat envied this Water Rites Master, who was idle all year round, frolicking in the mortal realm with a divine body.

On Waterfowl Island,

Chen Ping'an felt that from now on, he wouldn’t have a moment of idleness.

The Dao intent contained within the thirty-six green bricks had only just completed its first step, barely inviting the gods into the mountain and taking root in the mountain shrine. The next step of fully refining it into the mountain base was of utmost importance, otherwise, it would merely be a flower stand. However, the difficulty of refining Dao intent was even greater than peeling strands of water laws to transport to the water palace. This task consumed much more time; there were no shortcuts, only the slow and steady grinding of effort like dripping water through stone.

Chen Ping'an roughly estimated that completely refining the first green brick would take a full month, requiring at least six hours a day. Perhaps the refining of the remaining thirty-five bricks would become gradually faster, but at the very least, it would take two to three years of slow progress.

Moving the bricks up the mountain and transporting the water laws into the palace were long-term matters.

Fortunately, Chen Ping'an realized that he was practicing martial arts with some tendency toward mindless repetition, which allowed him to cultivate with reassurance under the identity of a qi refining cultivator.

In fact, he no longer needed to pursue a specific number of daily repetitions; as long as the intent of his fists flowed continuously, whether the bottleneck broke or not, he would allow things to happen naturally. As for whether he could reach the Golden Body realm as the strongest sixth realm, it wasn’t that he didn’t seek it, but he would no longer be overly demanding. If it came, it came; if it didn’t, then so be it. There was no need to practice the punching post relentlessly just to gain more martial fortune to present to Pei Qian. 

If he lost his way, how could he still teach the first disciple of the mountain?

When had he ever forced himself for martial fortune? Just because Pei Qian was your disciple, did he deserve such good fortune?

Moreover, Chen Ping'an had a vague feeling that after the martial fortune of Senior Gu You had dissipated, this strongest sixth realm would be difficult to attain. In truth, the gifts from Senior Gu and the martial fortune Chen Ping'an pursued were not necessarily connected, but the intricacies of life were hard to articulate. 

Furthermore, martial artists from the nine continents had their own opportunities and experiences, and Chen Ping'an wouldn’t dare to claim that he was the most pure.

The scene of the eighteen sword qi knocking on the last barrier was no longer something Chen Ping'an paid attention to.

The sharpening of the sword edge on the first and fifteenth day would eventually refine the two flying swords into life-bound objects, and there was no need to rush.

Next, while staying on Waterfowl Island, he still had to follow the old master’s advice and refine the abundant spiritual energy accumulated at the three critical energy points.

It was raining outside again.

Chen Ping'an thought for a moment and then stood up from the mat, holding an umbrella as he stepped outside.

The mountains and waters remained the same, and there were still issues to self-reflect on regarding his mindset. However, Chen Ping'an felt that he had one good thing: as long as he no longer found himself in a state of confusion, taking the first step was still something he could endure.

Chen Ping'an strolled slowly in the rain.

One fundamental matter, once understood, opens the door to all methods.

Clearing the clouds and mist to see the blue sky, and the bright moon.

With many flaws in his heart, he just needed to mend them.

For instance, having the heart to do good but not being rewarded is still good; if not rewarded, what does it matter? If the good fortune that falls upon others is not considered good fortune, then if one truly has the heart to do good but cannot amend more mistakes or accumulate merit for those wronged spirits, he should continue seeking ways to correct his mistakes. Over these years of going up mountains and down rivers, how many paths weren’t walked out through experience?

Chen Ping'an had always upheld the principle that a gentleman gives favors without seeking recompense. Was it merely to deceive himself and others? Once the same principle fell upon himself, did it make him uncomfortable?

This kind of self-deception with deep selfishness, if allowed to spread, would indeed lead to deceiving and harming others. Eventually, the so-called principles piled up behind his back would only make him increasingly unaware of his ignorance.

He resolved his mental knots.

His mindset lightened, but his shoulders felt heavy.

However, Chen Ping'an felt nothing amiss. He didn’t wear straw sandals, yet he remained Chen Ping'an. Among all the impoverished households in the world, there was one thing that didn’t need to be said: enduring hardship.

Only by enduring hardship can one enjoy blessings.
